## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task involves modeling population growth rate (dP/dt) as a function of time and current population size, which is a classic population ecology problem. The relationship likely involves density-dependent growth models where the growth rate depends on the current population level.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- {'name': 'Exponential (Malthusian) growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P', 'scenario': 'Unlimited resource, density-independent growth'}
- {'name': 'Logistic growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P)', 'scenario': 'Density-dependent growth with carrying capacity'}
- {'name': 'Gompertz growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P)', 'scenario': 'Growth rate decreases logarithmically as population approaches carrying capacity'}
- {'name': 'Theta-logistic growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2)', 'scenario': 'Generalized logistic with nonlinear density dependence'}
- {'name': 'Allee effect growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P)', 'scenario': 'Population with minimum viable population threshold (strong Allee effect)'}
- {'name': 'Richards growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) / c2', 'scenario': 'Asymmetric sigmoidal growth generalization'}
- {'name': 'Von Bertalanffy-type growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P', 'scenario': 'Balance between anabolic (power-law) and catabolic (linear) processes'}
- {'name': 'Power-law density dependence', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P**c1', 'scenario': 'Growth rate as a power function of population'}
- {'name': 'Beverton-Holt continuous analog', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) - c2 * P', 'scenario': 'Recruitment with density-dependent limitation minus mortality'}
- {'name': 'Time-dependent exponential growth', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t)', 'scenario': 'Growth rate with time-varying environmental conditions'}
- {'name': 'Logistic with time-varying rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * exp(c2 * t)', 'scenario': 'Density-dependent growth in changing environment'}
- {'name': 'Quadratic density dependence', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2', 'scenario': 'Taylor expansion of general density-dependent growth'}
- {'name': 'Cubic density dependence (weak Allee)', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3', 'scenario': 'Higher-order density effects including weak Allee effect'}

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent growth → multiplicative factor P*(1 - P/K) or P*f(P) where f decreases with P
- Allee effects (low-density decline) → cubic polynomial in P or product of two linear factors in P
- Carrying capacity saturation → growth rate changes sign at a critical population value, typically quadratic term with opposite sign
- Logarithmic density regulation → P*log(K/P) structure indicating Gompertz-type slow approach to equilibrium
- Metabolic scaling in growth → fractional power laws P**c with c between 0 and 1 representing allometric constraints
- Environmental stochasticity or temporal trends → multiplicative time-dependent modulation exp(c*t) or polynomial in t
- Competing anabolic vs catabolic processes → difference of power laws P**a - c*P**b with different exponents
- Zero growth at extinction → all growth rate terms should vanish when P=0, implying P appears as a factor in every term

I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) expression and compare it with each candidate.

**GT expression:**
$$f(P) = 0.9198(1 - P/84.03)P + 0.9198 \cdot P^2/(7.531P + 1)$$

Let me simplify:
$$f(P) = 0.9198P - 0.9198P^2/84.03 + 0.9198P^2/(7.531P + 1)$$
$$= 0.9198P - 0.01095P^2 + 0.9198P^2/(7.531P + 1)$$

Combining the last two terms over a common denominator:
$$= 0.9198P + \frac{-0.01095P^2(7.531P + 1) + 0.9198P^2}{7.531P + 1}$$
$$= 0.9198P + \frac{P^2(-0.08244P - 0.01095 + 0.9198)}{7.531P + 1}$$
$$= 0.9198P + \frac{P^2(0.9089 - 0.08244P)}{7.531P + 1}$$

Or combining everything over the common denominator $(7.531P + 1)$:
$$= \frac{0.9198P(7.531P + 1) + P^2(0.9089 - 0.08244P)}{7.531P + 1}$$
$$= \frac{6.927P^2 + 0.9198P + 0.9089P^2 - 0.08244P^3}{7.531P + 1}$$
$$= \frac{-0.08244P^3 + 7.836P^2 + 0.9198P}{7.531P + 1}$$
$$= \frac{P(-0.08244P^2 + 7.836P + 0.9198)}{7.531P + 1}$$

So the GT is a rational function of the form:
$$f(P) = \frac{aP^3 + bP^2 + cP}{dP + e}$$

This is key. The GT is a **cubic polynomial in P divided by a linear polynomial in P**, with no dependence on $t$.

Now let me check candidates that have this structure.
